## 📝 **SESSION ACCOMPLISHMENTS - JULY 29, 2025**

### **What We Completed Today**
1. **✅ Fixed "View Live Preview" Functionality**
   - Diagnosed issue: URLs pointed to fake .pages.dev domains
   - Implemented path-based routing: `/preview/business-name/design-type`
   - Updated WebsiteReplicator to generate correct worker domain URLs
   - Tested and confirmed both professional and science previews work

2. **✅ Integrated Firecrawl Throughout System**
   - Added Firecrawl API to WebsiteAnalyzer for better content extraction
   - Extended Firecrawl to WebsiteReplicator for consistent content processing
   - Added markdown processing for cleaner content understanding
   - Implemented intelligent fallback to basic HTTP when Firecrawl fails

3. **✅ Enhanced Content Processing**
   - Created `extractAllContentFromFirecrawl()` method
   - Added `extractTextContentFromMarkdown()` for markdown parsing
   - Improved business information extraction from combined sources
   - Better metadata extraction using Firecrawl's enhanced data

4. **✅ Deployment & Testing**
   - Successfully deployed version: b6921c72-b30c-4d36-960a-bbdfd98668f9
   - Tested full pipeline with example.com → Test Raw Dog Food Co
   - Verified preview URLs serve actual HTML content
   - Confirmed KV storage integration works correctly

```toml
[[env.production.kv_namespaces]]
binding = "WEBSITES_KV"
id = "4372765cc6554890bc082df7fbb3f225"

[[env.production.d1_databases]]
binding = "DB"
database_name = "findrawdogfood-db"
database_id = "9dcf8539-f274-486c-807b-7e265146ce6b"
```

## 🏗️ **SYSTEM ARCHITECTURE**

### **Core Components**
1. **Website Replicator** (`src/website-replicator.js`)
   - Fetches existing websites
   - Generates 2 modernized versions (Professional & Science-Backed)
   - Deploys to Cloudflare Pages

2. **SiteReviver Worker** (`src/sitereviver-worker.js`)
   - Main orchestrator service
   - Handles API requests
   - Coordinates screenshot generation and email templating

3. **🔥 Website Analyzer with Firecrawl** (`src/utils/website-analyzer.js`)
   - **NEW**: Firecrawl API integration for superior content extraction
   - Clean markdown conversion of website content
   - Enhanced metadata extraction (generator, viewport, etc.)
   - Intelligent fallback to basic HTTP if Firecrawl fails
   - Better modern website detection using framework metadata

4. **✅ Website Replicator with Firecrawl** (`src/website-replicator.js`)
   - **COMPLETED**: Integrated Firecrawl API for robust content extraction
   - Enhanced markdown processing for better content understanding
   - Improved business information extraction from clean content
   - Path-based preview URLs working: `/preview/business-name/design-type`
   - KV storage integration for serving generated websites

5. **Email Template System** (`src/rawgle-email-template.js`)
   - Production-ready Rawgle-branded emails
   - Based on `production_email_real-001.html` format
   - Static metrics with dynamic business data

6. **Integration Module** (`src/approval-dashboard-integration.js`)
   - Connects with existing approval dashboard
   - Enhanced UI with preview capabilities

### **Design Templates**
1. **🏢 Professional & Clean**
   - Conservative, trustworthy design
   - Blue/gray color scheme (#2b6cb0)
   - Clean navigation and typography

2. **🧠 Science-Backed UI**
   - Modern psychology-driven design
   - Dark theme with gradients (#0f1419)
   - F-pattern layouts and animations

## 🔌 **API ENDPOINTS**

### **POST /api/generate-email**
```bash
curl -X POST https://rawgle-sitereviver-prod.findrawdogfood.workers.dev/api/generate-email \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -d '{
    "websiteUrl": "https://example.com",
    "businessData": {
      "business_name": "Raw Dog Food Co",
      "city": "Seattle",
      "state": "WA", 
      "phone": "(555) 123-4567",
      "email": "info@example.com"
    }
  }'
```

### **POST /api/process-website**
```bash
curl -X POST https://rawgle-sitereviver-prod.findrawdogfood.workers.dev/api/process-website \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -d '{"websiteUrl": "https://example.com", "businessData": {...}}'
```

## 🚀 **DEPLOYMENT COMMANDS**

### **Production Deployment**
```bash
# Deploy to production
./deploy-sitereviver.sh production

# Or manual deployment
wrangler deploy --config wrangler-sitereviver.toml --env production

# Database schema setup
wrangler d1 execute findrawdogfood-db --file=database-schema-sitereviver.sql --remote
```

### **Development Commands**
```bash
# Local development
wrangler dev --config wrangler-sitereviver.toml --env development

# Database operations
npm run db:setup
npm run db:import
npm run db:reset
```

## 📊 **GENERATED WEBSITE URLS - ✅ WORKING**

### **Format**
- **Professional**: `https://rawgle-sitereviver-prod.findrawdogfood.workers.dev/preview/[business-name]/professional`
- **Science-Backed**: `https://rawgle-sitereviver-prod.findrawdogfood.workers.dev/preview/[business-name]/science`

### **Example Working URLs**
- **Professional**: `https://rawgle-sitereviver-prod.findrawdogfood.workers.dev/preview/test-raw-dog-food-co/professional`
- **Science**: `https://rawgle-sitereviver-prod.findrawdogfood.workers.dev/preview/test-raw-dog-food-co/science`

### **URL Sanitization**
```javascript
// Business name sanitization for URLs
function sanitizeName(name) {
    return name.toLowerCase()
        .replace(/[^a-z0-9\s-]/g, '')
        .replace(/\s+/g, '-')
        .replace(/-+/g, '-')
        .substring(0, 50);
}
```

## 🔍 **DEBUGGING & TROUBLESHOOTING**

### **Common Commands**
```bash
# View worker logs
wrangler tail rawgle-sitereviver-prod

# Check deployment status
wrangler deployments list --name rawgle-sitereviver-prod

# Test API endpoints
curl -s https://rawgle-sitereviver-prod.findrawdogfood.workers.dev

# Database queries
wrangler d1 execute findrawdogfood-db --command "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM sitereviver_results"
```

### **Error Patterns**
- **500 Errors**: Usually template variable issues
- **Database Timeouts**: Check D1 connection limits
- **KV Failures**: Verify namespace binding
- **Email Generation Fails**: Check business data format
